Absence of identical suit allows player to throw a card of another suit and the current round is won by highest card. Trump cards can be used to conquer other cards when no more cards of the same suit are there to offer. Trump card is by default Spade but you can set different trump suit like club, diamond or heart in this Call Break tash game.\r\n\r\nCall Break the term \"hand\" is used instead of trick, and \"Call\" is used instead of bid. After each deal player have to make a \"Call\" or \"bid\" for the number of hands he/she can capture, and the objective is to capture at least that many hand in a round, and try to break other player i.e. stop them from getting their Call.
